But fan fiction usually takes another authors characters and put them in a different situation If I have a choice between an original work or fan fiction, I'm paying for the original work. #amreading Since fan fiction  is being published these days, I feel like It should be stated. So I can make a informed decision. #amreading I'm not spending my hard earned money on a published booked that stemmed from someone else's hard work. #amreading Personally, I like fan fiction.
